+= \"<div class='thumbnail'>\";\n                product += \"<a href='\" + urlPrefix + data.Products[i].URL + \"'><img src='//images.backstreetmerch.com\" + data.Products[i].Img_URL +\"' id='thumbnail-product-slider' alt='Slide\" + i + \"'></a>\";\n                product += \"<div class='caption__product'>\";\n                product += \"<h3><a href='\" + urlPrefix + data.Products[i].Artist_URL + \"'>\"+ data.Products[i].Band_Name + \"</a></h3>\";\n                product += \"<p><a href='\" + urlPrefix + data.Products[i].URL + \"'>\"+ data.Products[i].ItemName + \"</a></p>\";\n\n                if  (data.Products[i].Currency==\"&euro;\") {\n                    product += \"<h3>PRICE:&nbsp;<a href='\" + data.Products[i].URL + \"'>\"+ FormatCurrency(data.Products[i].UnitPrice) +\" \"+ data.Products[i].Currency +\"</a></h3>\";\n                }\n                else {\n                    product += \"<h3>PRICE:&nbsp;<a href='\" + data.Products[i].URL + \"'>\"+ data.Products[i].Currency +\" \"+ FormatCurrency(data.Products[i].UnitPrice) +\"</a></h3>\";\n                }\n                product += \"<a href ='\" + data.Products[i].URL + \"' style='color:white' class = 'btn btn-custom-red'><i class='fa fa-shopping-cart'></i>&nbsp;Buy Now</a>\";\n                product += \"</div>\";\n                product += \"</div>\";\n                product += \"</div>\";\n            }\n            product += \"</div></div>\";\n            $(\"#TopItems\").append(product);\n        });\n\n\n\n        $(\"#hp_mens\").attr(\"href\",  urlPrefix +\"/advanced-search?#types=1&cats=&genres=&artists=&gender=2&sizes=&minprice=&maxprice=&pagesize=24&pageindex=1\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_womens\").attr(\"href\",  urlPrefix +\"/advanced-search?#types=1&cats=&genres=&artists=&gender=3&sizes=&minprice=&maxprice=&pagesize=24&pageindex=1\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_youth\").attr(\"href\",  urlPrefix +\"/advanced-search?#types=&cats=&genres=&artists=&gender=4&sizes=&minprice=&maxprice=&pagesize=24&pageindex=1\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_sale\").attr(\"href\",  urlPrefix +\"/search?search=nowonsale\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_vinyl\").attr(\"href\",  urlPrefix +\"/advanced-search?#types=3&cats=41&genres=&artists=&gender=&sizes=&minprice=&maxprice=&pagesize=24&pageindex=1#types=&cats=41&genres=&artists=&gender=&sizes=&minprice=&maxprice=&pagesize=24&pageindex=1\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_GiftVouchers\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/search?search=gift+vouchers\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_GiftVouchers_thumb\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/search?search=gift+vouchers\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_Alchemy2017\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/tag/alchemy\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_Alchemy2017_thumb\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/tag/alchemy\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_Anthrax\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/tag/among-the-kings-tour\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_Anthrax_thumb\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/tag/among-the-kings-tour\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_SpringSale\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/tag/spring-sale-2017\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_SpringSale_thumb\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/tag/spring-sale-2017\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_MetalSpring\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/tag/new-items\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_MetalSpring_thumb\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/tag/new-items\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_TheKinks\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/advanced-search?#types=&cats=&genres=&artists=2754&gender=&sizes=&minprice=&maxprice=&freeshipping=false&pagesize=24&pageindex=1\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_TheKinks_thumb\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/advanced-search?#types=&cats=&genres=&artists=2754&gender=&sizes=&minprice=&maxprice=&freeshipping=false&pagesize=24&pageindex=1\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_GhostPopestar\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/tag/ghost-popestar-tour-2017\");\n\n        $(\"#hp_GhostPopestar_thumb\").attr(\"href\", urlPrefix +\"/tag/ghost-popestar-tour-2017\");\n\n    });\n\n\n    function FormatCurrency(x) {\n        x = x.toFixed(2);\n        var retVal = x.toString().replace(/\\B(?=(\\d{3})+(?!\\d))/g, \",\");\n        return retVal;\n    };\n\n</script>\n\n\n\n
